          # I want the |horizontal| spacing between dashboard traffic

      204.

          # The start time will be the start time of the dojo.
        
      206. 
      
        
    206. 
          
          
          # The end time will be the current time.
        
      207. 
      
        
    207. 
          
          
          #
        
      208. 
      
        
    208. 
          
          
          # If there's lots of empty td's in a row (for all avatars)
        
      209.

      210.
